### [128] [Convergent Evolution: How Different Language Models Learn Similar Number Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20817)
*Deqing Fu,Tianyi Zhou,Mikhail Belkin,Vatsal Sharan,Robin Jia*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 语言模型在自然文本训练中学习使用周期特征表示数字，主要周期为2、5、10。研究发现这些特征存在两层层次结构：所有模型都学习到傅里叶域中具有周期T尖峰的特征，但只有部分模型学习到几何可分离特征，可用于线性分类数字模T。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是理解语言模型如何表示数字，特别是探索不同模型在数字表示学习中的共性和差异。虽然多种模型都学习到周期性的数字特征，但它们在几何可分离性方面表现不同，这促使研究者深入探究特征学习的机制和条件。

Method: 研究方法包括理论分析和实证研究。理论上证明了傅里叶域稀疏性是模T几何可分离的必要但不充分条件。实证上研究了不同因素对几何可分离特征学习的影响，包括数据、架构、优化器和分词器。通过分析互补共现信号和多标记加法问题来探索特征学习的途径。

Result: 研究发现：1）所有测试模型（Transformer、线性RNN、LSTM、经典词嵌入）都学习到傅里叶域中具有周期T尖峰的特征；2）只有部分模型学习到几何可分离特征；3）数据、架构、优化器和分词器都影响几何可分离特征的学习；4）模型可以通过两种途径获得几何可分离特征：从一般语言数据中的互补共现信号，或从多标记（非单标记）加法问题。

Conclusion: 结论表明特征学习存在趋同进化现象：各种不同的模型从不同的训练信号中学习到相似的特征。这揭示了语言模型数字表示学习的基本机制，并为理解模型如何从数据中提取结构化知识提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Language models trained on natural text learn to represent numbers using periodic features with dominant periods at $T=2, 5, 10$. In this paper, we identify a two-tiered hierarchy of these features: while Transformers, Linear RNNs, LSTMs, and classical word embeddings trained in different ways all learn features that have period-$T$ spikes in the Fourier domain, only some learn geometrically separable features that can be used to linearly classify a number mod-$T$. To explain this incongruity, we prove that Fourier domain sparsity is necessary but not sufficient for mod-$T$ geometric separability. Empirically, we investigate when model training yields geometrically separable features, finding that the data, architecture, optimizer, and tokenizer all play key roles. In particular, we identify two different routes through which models can acquire geometrically separable features: they can learn them from complementary co-occurrence signals in general language data, including text-number co-occurrence and cross-number interaction, or from multi-token (but not single-token) addition problems. Overall, our results highlight the phenomenon of convergent evolution in feature learning: A diverse range of models learn similar features from different training signals.

</details>


### [129] [Parallel-SFT: Improving Zero-Shot Cross-Programming-Language Transfer for Code RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20835)
*Zhaofeng Wu,Shiqi Wang,Boya Peng,Anuj Goyal,Melanie Kambadur,Sebastian Ruder,Yoon Kim,Chloe Bi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种通过并行SFT策略改善语言模型在不同编程语言间零样本迁移能力的方法，解决了RL训练在跨语言代码生成中的负迁移问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代语言模型在常见编程语言（如C++、Python）上表现出色，但在低资源编程语言上性能受限。虽然大多数编程技能在不同语言间是通用的，但研究发现RL训练在源语言上会降低模型在其他目标语言上的性能，存在负迁移问题。

Method: 提出Parallel-SFT策略，在SFT阶段将"并行程序"（功能相同但用多种编程语言实现的代码）纳入训练数据混合中。随后在Parallel-SFT模型上进行RL训练，以改善跨语言迁移能力。

Result: Parallel-SFT策略显著改善了跨语言迁移效果：在Parallel-SFT模型上进行RL训练后，模型在未见过的编程语言上表现出更好的泛化能力。模型内部表示分析显示，Parallel-SFT导致了一个更以功能为中心的潜在空间，不同语言中的等效程序更加紧密地聚集在一起。

Conclusion: 有效的RL跨语言迁移需要可泛化的SFT初始化。Parallel-SFT策略通过创建功能中心的表示空间，显著改善了语言模型在不同编程语言间的零样本迁移能力，为解决代码RL中的跨语言负迁移问题提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Modern language models demonstrate impressive coding capabilities in common programming languages (PLs), such as C++ and Python, but their performance in lower-resource PLs is often limited by training data availability. In principle, however, most programming skills are universal across PLs, so the capability acquired in one PL should transfer to others. In this work, we propose the task of zero-shot cross-programming-language transfer for code RL. We find that, for Llama-3.1, RL training for code generation in a source PL fails to improve, and sometimes even degrades, the performance on other target PLs. To address this, we hypothesize that effective RL transfer requires a generalizable SFT initialization before RL. We thus propose **Parallel-SFT**, an SFT strategy that incorporates "parallel programs" -- functionally equivalent code implemented in multiple PLs -- into the data mixture. We demonstrate that this improves transferability: when we subsequently perform RL on our Parallel-SFT model, we observe better generalization to unseen PLs. Analysis of the model internal representations reveals that Parallel-SFT leads to a more functionality-centric latent space, where equivalent programs across PLs are more tightly clustered, which we hypothesize to contribute to the improved transferability.

</details>


### [130] [SpeechParaling-Bench: A Comprehensive Benchmark for Paralinguistic-Aware Speech Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20842)
*Ruohan Liu,Shukang Yin,Tao Wang,Dong Zhang,Weiji Zhuang,Shuhuai Ren,Ran He,Caifeng Shan,Chaoyou Fu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SpeechParaling-Bench是一个用于副语言感知语音生成的综合基准，将特征覆盖从不到50个扩展到100多个细粒度特征，包含1000多个英中平行语音查询，通过基于LALM的成对比较评估缓解主观性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 副语言线索对于自然人机交互至关重要，但大型音频语言模型（LALMs）的评估受到粗粒度特征覆盖和评估主观性的限制，需要更全面的基准和可靠的评估方法。

Method: 1) 提出SpeechParaling-Bench基准，覆盖100多个细粒度副语言特征，包含1000多个英中平行语音查询，分为三个渐进挑战任务；2) 开发成对比较评估流程，使用基于LALM的评判器将候选响应与固定基线比较，通过相对偏好而非绝对评分缓解主观性。

Result: 实验显示当前LALMs存在显著局限：即使是领先的专有模型也难以实现全面的静态控制和副语言特征的动态调制；在情境对话中，43.3%的错误源于未能正确解释副语言线索。

Conclusion: 当前LALMs在副语言建模方面存在不足，需要更鲁棒的副语言建模方法以实现人类对齐的语音助手。

Abstract: Paralinguistic cues are essential for natural human-computer interaction, yet their evaluation in Large Audio-Language Models (LALMs) remains limited by coarse feature coverage and the inherent subjectivity of assessment. To address these challenges, we introduce SpeechParaling-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark for paralinguistic-aware speech generation. It expands existing coverage from fewer than 50 to over 100 fine-grained features, supported by more than 1,000 English-Chinese parallel speech queries, and is organized into three progressively challenging tasks: fine-grained control, intra-utterance variation, and context-aware adaptation. To enable reliable evaluation, we further develop a pairwise comparison pipeline, in which candidate responses are evaluated against a fixed baseline by an LALM-based judge. By framing evaluation as relative preference rather than absolute scoring, this approach mitigates subjectivity and yields more stable and scalable assessments without costly human annotation. Extensive experiments reveal substantial limitations in current LALMs. Even leading proprietary models struggle with comprehensive static control and dynamic modulation of paralinguistic features, while failure to correctly interpret paralinguistic cues accounts for 43.3% of errors in situational dialogue. These findings underscore the need for more robust paralinguistic modeling toward human-aligned voice assistants.

### [131] [Trust, Lies, and Long Memories: Emergent Social Dynamics and Reputation in Multi-Round Avalon with LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20582)
*Suveen Ellawela*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 研究LLM智能体在隐藏角色欺骗游戏《抵抗：阿瓦隆》中的涌现社会动态，重点关注重复游戏中的声誉形成和策略性欺骗行为


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注单次游戏表现，本研究旨在探索当LLM智能体在重复游戏中保留记忆时，社会动态如何演化，特别是声誉形成和策略性欺骗行为

Method: 让LLM智能体在《抵抗：阿瓦隆》游戏中重复进行188次游戏，智能体保留跨游戏记忆，包括角色分配和行为历史，研究不同推理努力水平下的行为差异

Result: 1. 跨游戏记忆促成了有机的声誉动态：智能体会参考过去行为，声誉具有角色条件性；高声誉玩家获得团队邀请增加46%
2. 高推理努力支持更策略性的欺骗：邪恶玩家更倾向于早期通过任务建立信任后再破坏（高努力75% vs 低努力36%）

Conclusion: 重复互动和记忆保留使LLM智能体产生了可测量的声誉和欺骗动态，表明LLM能够发展出复杂的社会行为模式，为研究多智能体社会互动提供了新视角

Abstract: We study emergent social dynamics in LLM agents playing The Resistance: Avalon, a hidden-role deception game. Unlike prior work on single-game performance, our agents play repeated games while retaining memory of previous interactions, including who played which roles and how they behaved, enabling us to study how social dynamics evolve. Across 188 games, two key phenomena emerge. First, reputation dynamics emerge organically when agents retain cross-game memory: agents reference past behavior in statements like "I am wary of repeating last game's mistake of over-trusting early success." These reputations are role-conditional: the same agent is described as "straightforward" when playing good but "subtle" when playing evil, and high-reputation players receive 46% more team inclusions. Second, higher reasoning effort supports more strategic deception: evil players more often pass early missions to build trust before sabotaging later ones, 75% in high-effort games vs 36% in low-effort games. Together, these findings show that repeated interaction with memory gives rise to measurable reputation and deception dynamics among LLM agents.

### [132] [Anchor-and-Resume Concession Under Dynamic Pricing for LLM-Augmented Freight Negotiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20732)
*Hoang Nguyen,Lu Wang,Marta Gaia Bras*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 提出两阶段锚定-恢复框架，通过价差推导的β参数适应动态定价，保证报价单调性，将LLM仅用作自然语言翻译层而非定价决策


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 货运经纪商在动态定价环境中面临挑战：传统固定β参数无法适应实时价格变化，而基于价差推导的β参数可能导致报价回撤违反单调性，LLM方案则存在成本高、非确定性和安全风险

Method: 提出两阶段锚定-恢复框架：1）基于价差推导自适应β参数，将每个货物的利润结构映射到正确的让步姿态；2）锚定-恢复机制保证在任意价格变动下报价单调非递减；LLM仅用作自然语言翻译层，定价决策保持确定性公式

Result: 在115,125次谈判中评估：窄价差时快速让步优先成交；中宽价差时匹配或超越最佳固定β基线；相比200亿参数LLM经纪商达成相似成交率和节省；对抗LLM驱动的承运商时保持可比节省和更高成交率

Conclusion: 该框架通过解耦LLM与定价逻辑，实现了可扩展的并发谈判处理、可忽略的推理成本和透明的决策过程，同时适应动态定价环境并保证报价单调性

Abstract: Freight brokerages negotiate thousands of carrier rates daily under dynamic pricing conditions where models frequently revise targets mid-conversation. Classical time-dependent concession frameworks use a fixed shape parameter $β$ that cannot adapt to these updates. Deriving $β$ from the live spread enables adaptation but introduces a new problem: a pricing shift can cause the formula to retract a previous offer, violating monotonicity. LLM-powered brokers offer flexibility but require expensive reasoning models, produce non-deterministic pricing, and remain vulnerable to prompt injection.
  We propose a two-index anchor-and-resume framework that addresses both limitations. A spread-derived $β$ maps each load's margin structure to the correct concession posture, while the anchor-and-resume mechanism guarantees monotonically non-decreasing offers under arbitrary pricing shifts. All pricing decisions remain in a deterministic formula; the LLM, when used, serves only as a natural-language translation layer. Empirical evaluation across 115,125 negotiations shows that the adaptive $β$ tailors behavior by regime: in narrow spreads, it concedes quickly to prioritize deal closure and load coverage; in medium and wide spreads, it matches or exceeds the best fixed-$β$ baselines in broker savings. Against an unconstrained 20-billion-parameter LLM broker, it achieves similar agreement rates and savings. Against LLM-powered carriers as more realistic stochastic counterparties, it maintains comparable savings and higher agreement rates than against rule-based opponents. By decoupling the LLM from pricing logic, the framework scales horizontally to thousands of concurrent negotiations with negligible inference cost and transparent decision-making.

</details>

### [133] [Statistical Software Engineering with Tuned Variables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19822)
*Nimrod Busany*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: AI系统维护的核心不是代码，而是版本化治理的程序空间，包含领域、结构约束、资格、评估资产和统计发布门控。AI系统在动态环境中运行，传统固定配置方法不足，应将选择视为受治理的调优变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI系统在动态环境中运行：提供商模型和API变化、输入分布漂移、评估集老化、质量/成本/延迟/安全等目标随时间重新协商。实践中团队常通过临时更改模型选择、检索策略、提示结构和操作阈值来应对，固定分配推理不足，因为选择的有效性取决于环境、评估集和政策状态。

Method: 将AI系统中的选择（如模型选择、检索策略、提示结构、操作阈值）视为受治理的调优变量，构建版本化治理的程序空间作为软件工程对象。基于统计方法，依赖抽样评估集、估计证据、效应量边界和置信度/风险阈值进行发布决策。

Result: 提出将治理空间作为软件工程对象的新视角，强调AI系统维护需要动态的、受治理的调优方法，而非传统的固定配置。统计发布门控确保决策基于可靠证据。

Conclusion: AI系统维护应转向版本化治理的程序空间方法，将关键选择作为受治理的调优变量管理，以适应动态环境和评估集的演变，确保系统在变化条件下的可靠性和有效性。

Abstract: The maintained artifact in an AI-enabled system is not code plus settings, but a versioned governed program space: domains, structural constraints, eligibility, evaluation assets, and a statistical release gate. AI-enabled systems operate under changing world conditions: provider models and APIs change, input distributions drift, evaluation sets age, and objectives such as quality, cost, latency, and safety are renegotiated over time. In practice, teams often respond through ad hoc changes to model choice, retrieval policy, prompt structure, and operational thresholds. Fixed-assignment reasoning is therefore insufficient: a chosen assignment is valid only relative to an environment, evaluation set, and policy state. We argue that such choices should be treated as tuned variables: program variables maintained under governance as environments and evaluation sets evolve. Building on SE4AI work and our prior work on governed tuning, this paper positions the governed space as the software-engineering object. Here, statistical means that promotion relies on sampled evaluation sets, estimated evidence, effect-size margins, and confidence/risk thresholds.

</details>


### [134] [Stateful Embedded Fuzzing with Peripheral-Accurate SystemC Virtual Prototypes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19824)
*Chiara Ghinami,Igor Pontes Tresolavy,Luis Seibt,Nils Bosbach,Rainer Leupers*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出一个集成AFL++与SystemC-TLM虚拟原型的新框架，用于嵌入式软件的逼真模糊测试，解决了现有方法在嵌入式环境中外围设备行为模拟不足的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 嵌入式软件复杂度增加使得手动测试不切实际，需要自动化测试技术。现有覆盖引导模糊测试工具（如AFL++）在嵌入式环境中应用困难，因为外围设备行为对嵌入式系统至关重要。现有方法要么使用快速用户模式模拟器但牺牲外围设备真实性，要么依赖全系统模拟器但需要手动插装，限制了大规模软件的应用。

Method: 提出一个新颖框架，将AFL++与状态化SystemC-TLM虚拟原型集成，实现嵌入式软件的逼真模糊测试。模糊测试生成的输入直接注入到外围设备模型中，使外围设备能够触发自然副作用（如中断和FIFO更新）。通过将模糊测试与全系统模拟集成，该框架提升了嵌入式系统硅前测试的有效性。

Result: 在嵌入式工作负载上的结果显示，该方法消除了误报，同时保持了与最先进工具相当的代码覆盖率和执行性能。

Conclusion: 通过集成AFL++与SystemC-TLM虚拟原型，该框架实现了嵌入式软件的逼真模糊测试，解决了现有方法在嵌入式环境中外围设备行为模拟不足的问题，提升了嵌入式系统硅前测试的有效性。

Abstract: The increasing complexity of embedded software has made comprehensive manual testing impractical, motivating the use of automated techniques such as fuzzing. Coverage-guided fuzzers like AFL++ have shown strong results for conventional software but remain challenging to apply effectively in embedded contexts, where peripheral behaviors play critical roles. Existing approaches either use fast user-mode simulators, sacrificing peripheral realism, or rely on full-system simulators with manual instrumentation, limiting applicability to large-scale software. In this work, we present a novel framework that integrates AFL++ with a stateful SystemC-TLM virtual prototype to enable realistic fuzzing of embedded software. Fuzzer-generated inputs are injected directly into peripheral models, allowing peripherals to trigger natural side effects such as interrupts and FIFO updates. By integrating fuzzing with full-system simulation, our framework advances the effectiveness of pre-silicon testing for embedded systems. Results on embedded workloads show that our approach eliminates false positives while maintaining comparable code coverage and execution performance as state-of-the-art tools.

</details>


### [135] [SolidCoder: Bridging the Mental-Reality Gap in LLM Code Generation through Concrete Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19825)
*Woojin Lee,Jin-Xia Huang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: SolidCoder提出S.O.L.I.D.架构解决代码生成中的"心智-现实鸿沟"，通过强制边缘情况意识和沙箱执行验证，在多个基准测试中实现SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码生成框架依赖心智模拟，但存在"心智-现实鸿沟"：模型会幻觉执行轨迹并自信地验证有缺陷的代码。这一鸿沟表现为两个正交维度：规范鸿沟（规划时忽略边缘情况）和验证鸿沟（为有缺陷代码幻觉正确行为）。

Method: 提出SolidCoder，核心原则是"不要想象，要执行"。S.O.L.I.D.架构通过两个关键组件解决这两个维度：1）在算法设计前强制边缘情况意识；2）用沙箱执行和基于属性的预言机替代想象中的轨迹验证。

Result: 使用GPT-4o时，SolidCoder在HumanEval上达到95.7% pass@1（+0.6%p），CodeContests上77.0%（+4.3%p），APPS上26.7%（+3.4%p），均实现SOTA性能。消融实验显示边缘情况意识提供最大个体增益，而执行基础能捕捉规范改进无法解决的类别不同错误。

Conclusion: 解决规范鸿沟和验证鸿沟对于稳健的代码合成至关重要。SolidCoder的增益可泛化到RL后训练模型，表明同时解决两个鸿沟维度是代码生成的关键。作者发布了代码和框架以促进未来研究。

Abstract: State-of-the-art code generation frameworks rely on mental simulation, where LLMs internally trace execution to verify correctness. We expose a fundamental limitation: the Mental-Reality Gap -- where models hallucinate execution traces and confidently validate buggy code. This gap manifests along two orthogonal dimensions: the Specification Gap (overlooking edge cases during planning) and the Verification Gap (hallucinating correct behavior for flawed code). We propose SolidCoder with a simple principle: don't imagine -- execute. The S.O.L.I.D. architecture addresses both dimensions by forcing edge-case awareness before algorithm design and replacing imagined traces with sandboxed execution using property-based oracles. With GPT-4o, SolidCoder achieves state-of-the-art pass@1 performance: 95.7% on HumanEval (+0.6%p), 77.0% on CodeContests (+4.3%p), and 26.7% on APPS (+3.4%p). Ablation reveals that edge-case awareness provides the largest individual gain, while execution grounding catches categorically different errors that specification improvements cannot address. These gains generalize to RL post-trained models, validating that bridging both gap dimensions is essential for robust code synthesis. We release our code and framework to facilitate future research.

</details>


### [136] [Co-Located Tests, Better AI Code: How Test Syntax Structure Affects Foundation Model Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19826)
*Éric Jacopin*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究比较了内联测试（Python doctests）与分离测试（Rust #[test]块）对AI代码生成质量的影响，发现内联测试在代码保持性和正确性方面表现显著更好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI编码助手越来越多地生成代码和测试，测试代码的结构（内联实现还是分离块）传统上是测试哲学问题。本研究旨在探究这种选择是否影响AI代码生成质量。

Method: 使用SEGA三维评估框架（确定性、保持性、正确性）进行大规模实证研究（830+生成文件，12个模型，3个提供商）。比较Python doctests（内联测试语法）和Rust #[test]块（分离测试语法）在d-ary堆实现上的表现。对7个开源架构（6个Transformer和1个门控线性RNN）进行机制分析。

Result: 1) 内联测试在所有模型中实现近乎完美的保持性（100%）和正确性（92-100%）；2) 分离测试暴露明显的模型层级差距（0-100%正确性），且保持性与正确性相互独立；3) 模型行为随代际演变，一个模型打破了其三个前身的测试抑制模式；4) 机制分析显示内联测试标记在5/7模型中接收2.8-4.4倍更强的注意力，因果验证通过敲除和引导实验确认，该机制扩展到非Transformer架构。

Conclusion: 在基础模型时代，测试语法结构是软件设计的重要考量：将测试与实现代码共置能产生可测量更好的AI生成代码。该设计建议对未来架构变化具有鲁棒性。

Abstract: AI coding assistants increasingly generate code alongside tests. How developers structure test code, whether inline with the implementation or in separate blocks, has traditionally been a matter of testing philosophy. We investigate whether this choice affects AI code generation quality.
  We conduct a large-scale empirical study (830+ generated files, 12 models, 3 providers) using SEGA, a three-dimensional evaluation framework measuring Determinism, Preservation, and Correctness. Comparing inline test syntax (Python doctests) against separated test syntax (Rust #[test] blocks) on a d-ary heap implementation, we find that: (1) inline tests yield near-perfect preservation (100%) and correctness (92-100%) across all models; (2) separated tests expose stark model-tier gaps (0-100% correctness) and independence between preservation and correctness; (3) model behavior evolves across generations, and notably one model breaks the test suppression pattern of its three predecessors; (4) mechanistic analysis on 7 open-source architectures (6 transformers and a gated-linear Recurrent Neural Network (RNN)) reveals inline test markers receive 2.8-4.4$\times$ stronger attention in 5/7 models, with causal validation via knockout and steering experiments on the 4 code-specialized transformers and RWKV-6; the co-location mechanism extends to a non-transformer architecture, suggesting the design recommendation is robust to future architectural shifts. In the Foundation Model era, test syntax structure is a software design concern: co-locating tests with implementation code produces measurably better AI-generated code. This arxiv long version includes appendices that further qualify the effect as bounded by both model capability and programming language.

</details>


### [137] [More Is Different: Toward a Theory of Emergence in AI-Native Software Ecosystems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19827)
*Daniel Russo*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文认为AI原生软件生态系统应被视为复杂适应系统(CAS)，而非传统软件架构，因为多智能体AI系统的故障模式无法用现有理论解释。论文提出了测量因果涌现的框架和七个可证伪命题，挑战了软件工程的核心假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统软件工程理论无法解释多智能体AI系统的故障模式：单个智能体运行正常，但它们的交互却导致整个生态系统退化。这揭示了我们对软件演化理解上的空白，需要新的理论框架来研究AI原生软件生态系统。

Method: 1. 将AI原生软件生态系统建模为复杂适应系统(CAS)，将Holland的六个CAS属性映射到可观察的生态系统动态；2. 定义测量因果涌现的框架：微观状态变量、粗粒度函数和可处理的测量方法；3. 提出七个可证伪命题，将CAS理论与软件演化联系起来，挑战或扩展Lehman定律。

Result: 论文提出了一个理论框架，能够解释AI原生软件生态系统中出现的涌现特性，如架构熵、级联故障和理解债务。这些特性源于智能体间的交互，而非单个组件。如果命题被证实，将需要根本性的转变：生态系统级监控成为AI原生系统的主要治理机制。

Conclusion: AI原生软件生态系统必须作为复杂适应系统来研究，这挑战了软件工程的核心假设。无论七个命题被证实还是证伪，这项工作都迫使软件工程领域重新思考：在自主智能体时代，软件工程的基本假设是否还能成立？

Abstract: Software engineering faces a fundamental challenge: multi-agent AI systems fail in ways that defy explanation by traditional theories. While individual agents perform correctly, their interactions degrade entire ecosystems, revealing a gap in our understanding of software evolution. This paper argues that AI-native software ecosystems must be studied as complex adaptive systems (CAS), where emergent properties like architectural entropy, cascade failures, and comprehension debt arise not from individual components, but from their interactions. We map Holland's six CAS properties onto observable ecosystem dynamics, distinguishing these systems from microservices or open-source networks. To measure causal emergence, we define micro-level state variables, coarse-graining functions, and a tractable measurement framework. Seven falsifiable propositions link CAS theory to software evolution, challenging or extending Lehman's laws where agent-level assumptions fail. If confirmed, these findings would demand a radical shift: ecosystem-level monitoring as the primary governance mechanism for AI-native systems. If refuted, existing theories may only need incremental updates. Either way, this work forces us to ask: Can software engineering's core assumptions survive the age of autonomous agents?

</details>


### [138] [ViBR: Automated Bug Replay from Video-based Reports using Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19905)
*Sidong Feng,Dingbang Wang,Nikola Tomic,Tingting Yu,Aldeida Aleti,Chunyang Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GUI屏幕录制视频作为bug报告工具越来越流行，但现有方法依赖脆弱的图像处理启发式方法、显式触摸指示器或预构建的UI转换图，需要复杂的仪器化和应用特定设置，自动从录屏中复现bug仍然是一个重大挑战。

Method: ViBR结合基于CLIP的嵌入相似性进行动作边界分割，使用视觉语言模型进行区域感知GUI状态比较和引导bug重放，是一个轻量级全自动方法。

Result: 实验结果显示ViBR成功复现了72%的bug录屏，显著优于最先进的基准方法和消融变体。

Conclusion: ViBR提供了一种有效的方法来自动化从GUI录屏中复现bug，克服了现有方法的局限性，在bug复现方面取得了显著改进。

Abstract: Bug reports play a critical role in software maintenance by helping users convey encountered issues to developers. Recently, GUI screen capture videos have gained popularity as a bug reporting artifact due to their ease of use and ability to retain rich contextual information. However, automatically reproducing bugs from such recordings remains a significant challenge. Existing methods often rely on fragile image-processing heuristics, explicit touch indicators, or pre-constructed UI transition graphs, which require non-trivial instrumentation and app-specific setup. This paper presents ViBR, a lightweight and fully automated approach that reproduces bugs directly from GUI recordings. Specifically, ViBR combines CLIP-based embedding similarity for action boundary segmentation with Vision-Language Models (VLMs) for region-aware GUI state comparison and guided bug replay. Experimental results show that ViBR successfully reproduces 72% of bug recordings, significantly outperforming state-of-the-art baselines and ablation variants.

Abstract: In this paper, we conduct a systematic literature review of (semi-) automated approaches to Quantum Software Engineering (QSE) and Quantum Artificial Intelligence (QAI). This also holds in the Quantum Computing (QC), Quantum Information Science (QIS), and Quantum Engineering (QE) world, as well as in hybrid quantum-classical applications. This can be a significant help to achieve productivity leap and efficiency even for subject matter experts. Unlike prior literature reviews and surveys, this work focuses on automation in SE and AI for quantum and hybrid quantum-classical applications and identifies the recent trends and future directions through a systematic literature review. We are interested in methods and techniques that can enable a broader development and deployment of quantum and hybrid AI-enabled software systems.

### [140] [FIKA: Expanding Dependency Reachability with Executability Guarantees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20015)
*Yogya Gamage,Meriem Ben Chaaben,Martin Monperrus,Benoit Baudry*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: FIKA是一个用于提供第三方库调用点可执行性保证的管道，通过生成可执行代码并分析执行轨迹来验证调用点的实际可达性，相比现有测试套件能提高20%的覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的依赖可达性分析工具大多是静态的，受限于缺乏实际执行验证。需要一种能够提供第三方库调用点可执行性保证的方法，以提高依赖管理的精确性。

Method: FIKA通过生成可执行代码并分析其执行轨迹来验证第三方库调用点的实际可达性。该方法为每个调用点创建可执行代码，运行这些代码，并通过执行轨迹提供可执行性保证。

Result: 在8个Java项目数据集上，现有测试套件平均覆盖54%的调用点，FIKA进一步提高了20%的覆盖率，能够为2363个依赖方法提供可执行性证明。在6个项目中，FIKA为超过75%的调用点提供了强可执行性保证。FIKA还能改进Semgrep等静态漏洞可达性分析工具的结果，帮助优先处理具有更强可执行性保证的漏洞更新。

Conclusion: FIKA通过动态执行验证有效提高了第三方库调用点的可执行性覆盖率，为依赖管理提供了更精确的可达性分析，能够改进现有静态分析工具的结果并帮助优先处理漏洞更新。

Abstract: Automated third-party library analysis tools help developers by addressing key dependency management challenges, such as automating version updates, detecting vulnerabilities, and detecting breaking updates. Dependency reachability analysis aims at improving the precision of dependency management, by reducing the space of dependency issues to the ones that actually matter. Most tools for dependency reachability analysis are static and fundamentally limited by the absence of execution. In this paper, we propose FIKA, a pipeline for providing guarantees of executability for third-party library call sites. FIKA generates code that is executed, and whose execution trace provides guarantees that a third-party library call site is actually reachable. We apply our approach to a dataset of eight Java projects to empirically evaluate the effectiveness of FIKA. On average, 54% of these call sites are covered by the existing test suites, and therefore, have evidence for their executability. FIKA further improves this coverage by 20% and is able to demonstrate executability for 2363 dependency methods. In six out of eight projects, FIKA provides strong guarantees that more than 75% of call sites are executable. We further demonstrate that FIKA is capable of improving the results provided by Semgrep, a state-of-the-art static vulnerability reachability analysis tool. We show that FIKA can help prioritize the vulnerability updates with stronger guarantees of executability in cases where Semgrep yields inconclusive reachability results.

</details>


### [141] [Hallucination Inspector: A Fact-Checking Judge for API Migration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20202)
*Marcos Tileria,Santanu Kumar Dash,Profir-Petru Pârţachi,Earl T. Barr*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出Hallucination Inspector工具，用于检测LLM在API迁移任务中产生的"脚手架幻觉"问题，即模型生成不存在的API符号调用代码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在自动化软件工程任务（如API迁移）中经常产生"脚手架幻觉"，即生成调用不存在API符号（如虚构的导入、构造函数、常量）的错误代码，而标准评估指标无法有效检测这种问题。

Method: 提出Hallucination Inspector静态分析工具，通过轻量级评估框架验证从抽象语法树提取的符号，与直接从API软件文档构建的知识库进行比对。

Result: 在Android API迁移任务上的初步评估表明，该方法成功识别了幻觉现象，相比标准指标和概率判断器显著减少了误报。

Conclusion: 需要专门工具来检测LLM在代码生成中的脚手架幻觉问题，Hallucination Inspector提供了一种有效的静态分析方法。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in automated software engineering for tasks such as API migration. While LLMs are able to identify migration patterns, they often make mistakes and fail to produce correct glue code to invoke the new API in place of the old one. We call this issue Scaffolding Hallucination, a failure mode where models generate incorrect calling contexts by inventing Phantom Symbols -- such as imaginary imports, constructors, and constants -- that do not exist in the API specification. In this paper, we show that standard metrics cannot be relied upon to detect these instances of hallucination. We propose Hallucination Inspector, a static analysis tool to detect Scaffolding Hallucination in LLM-generated code. Our approach includes a lightweight evaluation framework that verifies symbols extracted from the abstract syntax tree against a knowledge base derived directly from software documentation for the API. A preliminary evaluation on Android API migrations demonstrates that our approach successfully identifies hallucinations and significantly reduces false positives compared to standard metrics and probabilistic judges

### [142] [Towards Secure Logging: Characterizing and Benchmarking Logging Code Security Issues with LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20211)
*He Yang Yuan,Xin Wang,Kundi Yao,An Ran Chen,Zishuo Ding,Zhenhao Li*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文系统分析了日志代码的安全问题，构建了包含4类10种模式的分类体系，创建了包含101个真实案例的基准数据集，并评估了LLM在检测和修复日志安全问题上的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 日志代码在软件系统中记录关键事件和行为，对调试和监控至关重要，但不安全的日志实践可能暴露敏感信息或引发攻击。现有研究主要关注日志代码的一般缺陷，对安全问题的系统分析有限，特别是利用LLM进行检测和修复的研究不足。

Method: 1) 构建了包含4个常见问题类别和10个相应模式的日志代码安全问题分类体系；2) 创建了包含101个真实世界日志安全问题报告的基准数据集；3) 提出了一个自动化框架，整合多种上下文知识来评估LLM在检测和修复日志安全问题上的能力。

Result: 实验结果显示：1) LLM在检测安全问题方面表现中等（准确率平均在12.9%到52.5%之间）；2) LLM在可靠生成正确代码修复方面面临明显挑战；3) 仅使用问题描述比安全模式解释或两者结合更能提高LLM的检测准确率。

Conclusion: 研究结果为从业者提供了可行的见解，并突出了当前LLM在安全日志记录方面的潜力和局限性。LLM在检测日志安全问题方面有一定效果，但在可靠修复方面仍需改进。

Abstract: Logging code plays an important role in software systems by recording key events and behaviors, which are essential for debugging and monitoring. However, insecure logging practices can inadvertently expose sensitive information or enable attacks such as log injection, posing serious threats to system security and privacy. Prior research has examined general defects in logging code, but systematic analysis of logging code security issues remains limited, particularly in leveraging LLMs for detection and repair. In this paper, we derive a comprehensive taxonomy of logging code security issues, encompassing four common issue categories and 10 corresponding patterns. We further construct a benchmark dataset with 101 real-world logging security issue reports that have been manually reviewed and annotated. We then propose an automated framework that incorporates various contextual knowledge to evaluate LLMs' capabilities in detecting and repairing logging security issues. Our experimental results reveal a notable disparity in performance: while LLMs are moderately effective at detecting security issues (e.g., the accuracy ranges from 12.9% to 52.5% on average), they face noticeable challenges in reliably generating correct code repairs. We also find that the issue description alone improves the LLMs' detection accuracy more than the security pattern explanation or a combination of both. Overall, our findings provide actionable insights for practitioners and highlight the potential and limitations of current LLMs for secure logging.

</details>


### [143] [On the Informativeness of Security Commit Messages: A Large-scale Replication Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20461)
*Syful Islam,Stefano Zacchiroli*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究复制并扩展了Reis等人(2023)关于安全相关提交信息信息量的研究，确认了原始发现：安全相关提交信息普遍信息量不足，且随时间推移情况在恶化。研究还发现不同软件生态系统间存在显著差异，并意外发现符合Conventional Commits规范的提交信息量更低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证Reis等人(2023)关于安全相关提交信息信息量不足的研究结果的稳健性，并通过独立复制和扩展研究来更全面地理解这一现象。

Method: 1. 独立复制研究：不使用原始研究的任何数据或分析流程，仅基于论文描述重新实现方法；2. 检索50,673个安全相关提交；3. 使用与原始研究相同的时间段(1999年6月至2022年8月)和来源(GitHub)；4. 扩展研究：延长时间段至2025年10月，按软件生态系统(如Linux内核、Ubuntu、Go、PyPI等)细分分析，并评估Conventional Commits规范的影响。

Result: 1. 成功复制了原始研究的负面结果：安全相关提交信息普遍信息量不足，统计显著；2. 在更长的时间段内，提交信息的信息量在恶化；3. 不同软件生态系统间存在显著的信息量差异；4. 意外发现：符合Conventional Commits规范的提交比不符合的信息量更低。

Conclusion: 需要跨生态系统分析来理解平台和社区特定的提交信息实践，并制定普遍适用的安全相关提交信息编写指南。当前的安全相关提交信息普遍信息量不足，且某些"最佳实践"可能适得其反。

Abstract: The informativeness of security-related commit messages is crucial for patch triage: when high, it enables the rapid distribution and deployment of security fixes. Prior research (Reis et al., 2023) reported, however, that commit messages are often too uninformative to support these activities. To assess the robustness of this negative result, we independently replicate the original study using only the information provided in the paper, without reusing any of the original artifacts (data, analysis pipeline, etc.). We retrieve \num{50673} security-related commits and analyze their informativeness using an independent re-implementation of the techniques introduced by Reis et al. For the same source (i.e., GitHub) and time period (from June 1999 to August 2022) as the original study, our replication confirms the original findings in a statistically significant way: security-related commit messages are, in general, not informative enough for security-focused purposes. We then extend the original study in several ways. Over a longer time period (from June 1999 to October 2025), we find that commit-message informativeness is worsening. Breaking results down by software ecosystem (Linux kernel, Ubuntu, Go, PyPI, etc.), we observe significant differences in informativeness. Finally, we examine emerging best practices for writing commit messages, such as the Conventional Commits Specification (CCS), and again find significant differences in an unexpected direction: CCS-compliant commits are less informative than non-compliant ones. Our findings highlight the need for cross-ecosystem analyses to understand platform- and community-specific commit-message practices, and to inform the development and adoption of universally applicable guidelines for writing informative security-related commit messages.

</details>


### [144] [Finding Duplicates in 1.1M BDD Steps: cukereuse, a Paraphrase-Robust Static Detector for Cucumber and Gherkin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20462)
*Ali Hassaan Mughal,Noor Fatima,Muhammad Bilal*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 开发了cukereuse工具，通过静态分析检测BDD测试中的步骤文本重复，结合哈希、编辑距离和语义嵌入技术，在347个GitHub仓库中识别出高重复率（80.2%），并提供开源工具和数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有BDD重复检测方法需要运行测试或局限于单个组织，缺乏静态、抗释义、可在任何代码库使用的步骤级检测工具。

Method: 开发cukereuse开源Python CLI工具，采用分层管道结合精确哈希、Levenshtein比率和句子转换器嵌入技术，分析347个公开GitHub仓库的23,667个.feature文件和1,113,616个Gherkin步骤。

Result: 步骤加权精确重复率为80.2%，仓库中位数重复率为58.6%；最强混合聚类包含20.7k次出现分布在2.2k个文件中；在人工标注的1,020对样本上，无分数标注的F1=0.822，主要标注的语义F1=0.906；同时使用CDN框架对Gherkin语言进行了批判性分析。

Conclusion: 填补了静态、抗释义、跨仓库BDD步骤重复检测的空白，提供开源工具、语料库和标注数据，揭示了Gherkin语言在八个认知维度上的问题。

Abstract: Behaviour-Driven Development (BDD) suites accumulate step-text duplication whose
  maintenance cost is established in prior work. Existing detection techniques require
  running the tests (Binamungu et al., 2018-2023) or are confined to a single
  organisation (Irshad et al., 2020-2022), leaving a gap: a purely static,
  paraphrase-robust, step-level detector usable on any repository. We fill the gap
  with cukereuse, an open-source Python CLI combining exact hashing, Levenshtein
  ratio, and sentence-transformer embeddings in a layered pipeline, released alongside
  an empirical corpus of 347 public GitHub repositories, 23,667 parsed .feature
  files, and 1,113,616 Gherkin steps. The step-weighted exact-duplicate rate is 80.2
  %; the median-repository rate is 58.6 % (Spearman rho = 0.51 with size). The top
  hybrid cluster groups 20.7k occurrences across 2.2k files. Against 1,020 pairs
  manually labelled by the three authors under a released rubric (inter-annotator
  Fleiss' kappa = 0.84 on a 60-pair overlap), we report precision, recall, and F1 with
  bootstrap 95 % CIs under two protocols: the primary rubric and a score-free
  second-pass relabelling. The strongest honest pair-level number is near-exact at F1
  = 0.822 on score-free labels; the primary-rubric semantic F1 = 0.906 is inflated by
  a stratification artefact that pins recall at 1.000. Lexical baselines
  (SourcererCC-style, NiCad-style) reach primary F1 = 0.761 and 0.799. The paper also
  presents a CDN-structured critique of Gherkin (Cognitive Dimensions of Notations);
  eight of fourteen dimensions are rated problematic or unsupported. The tool, corpus,
  labelled pairs, rubric, and pipeline are released under permissive licences.

</details>

### [146] [DeepParse: Hybrid Log Parsing with LLM-Synthesized Regex Masks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20553)
*Amir Shetaia,Sean Kauffman*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: DeepParse是一个混合日志解析框架，使用LLM从小样本中挖掘可重用变量模式，然后通过Drain算法确定性应用，实现高精度、可扩展且成本高效的日志结构化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代分布式系统产生大量异构日志，但日志解析面临格式演进和标记数据有限的挑战。基于机器学习的解析器（如Drain）速度快但复杂变量精度下降，而LLM泛化能力强但推理成本过高。

Method: DeepParse采用混合框架：首先使用LLM从小样本日志中自动挖掘可重用变量模式，然后将这些模式通过Drain算法确定性应用，将推理阶段与执行阶段分离。

Result: 在16个基准数据集上，DeepParse在变量提取方面达到97.6%的平均解析精度，比启发式和纯LLM基线表现更好。集成到异常检测管道中，相比启发式基线减少30%以上误报，推理延迟降低36%。

Conclusion: DeepParse通过分离推理与执行，实现了准确、可扩展且成本高效的日志结构化，无需依赖脆弱的手工规则或每行神经推理，在精度和效率方面均优于现有方法。

Abstract: Modern distributed systems produce massive, heterogeneous logs essential for reliability, security, and anomaly detection. Converting these free-form messages into structured templates (log parsing) is challenging due to evolving formats and limited labeled data. Machine-learning-based parsers like Drain are fast but accuracy often degrades on complex variables, while Large Language Models (LLMs) offer better generalization but incur prohibitive inference costs. This paper presents DeepParse, a hybrid framework that automatically mines reusable variable patterns from small log samples using an LLM, then applies them deterministically through the Drain algorithm. By separating the reasoning phase from execution, DeepParse enables accurate, scalable, and cost-efficient log structuring without relying on brittle handcrafted rules or per-line neural inference. Across 16 benchmark datasets, DeepParse achieves higher accuracy in variable extraction (97.6% average Parsing Accuracy) and better consistency than both heuristic and LLM-only baselines. Integrating DeepParse into an anomaly detection pipeline reduced false alarms by over 30% and reduced inference latency by 36% compared to heuristic baselines.

### [147] [Evaluating Software Defect Prediction Models via the Area Under the ROC Curve Can Be Misleading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20742)
*Luigi Lavazza,Gabriele Rotoloni,Sandro Morasca*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文挑战了传统观点，指出高AUC值并不能保证软件缺陷预测模型在所有阈值下都比随机模型表现更好，需要装饰ROC曲线或替代表示来全面评估模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是调查基于ROC曲线和AUC的软件缺陷预测模型评估是否可靠。传统观点认为完全位于ROC空间对角线之上的ROC曲线优于随机模型，高AUC值代表良好性能，但作者质疑这些信念是否正确。

Method: 方法包括：1）装饰ROC曲线，突出显示对应阈值值的点；2）将真阳性率和假阳性率表示为阈值的函数。通过这些方法，可以评估模型是否在所有阈值下都比随机模型更好地分类故障和非故障模块。

Result: 结果表明，常用的评估标准可能导致错误结论。高AUC值并不能保证模型在所有可能阈值下的真阳性率和假阳性率都优于随机模型。

Conclusion: 结论是：需要装饰ROC曲线或替代表示来全面评估软件缺陷预测模型的所有相关方面。仅依赖传统ROC曲线和AUC评估可能产生误导性结果。

Abstract: Background: Receiver Operating Characteristic (ROC) curves are widely used to evaluate the performance of Software Defect Prediction (SDP) models that estimate module fault-proneness, i.e., the probability that a module is faulty. A ROC curve maps a model's performance in terms of True Positive Rate and False Positive Rate for any possible threshold set on fault-proneness. The Area Under the ROC Curve (AUC) summarizes the performance of a model across all possible thresholds. Traditionally, ROC curves completely above the bisector of the ROC space are considered better than random, and high AUC values are associated with good performance. Aim: We investigate whether these beliefs are correct, hence if SDP model evaluation based on ROC curves and AUC is reliable. Method: We decorate ROC curves by highlighting the points corresponding to threshold values. We also represent True Positive Rate and False Positive Rate as functions of the threshold. Thus, we can evaluate whether a model classifies both faulty and non-faulty modules better than the random model. Results: We show that commonly used evaluation criteria may lead to wrong conclusions. Conclusions: A high value of AUC does not guarantee that both the True Positive Rate and the False Positive Rate of a model are better than the random model's for all possible thresholds. Either decorated ROC curves or alternative representations are needed to appreciate all the relevant aspects of SDP models.

</details>

Abstract: Introductory Software Engineering (SE) courses face rapidly increasing student enrollment numbers, participants with diverse backgrounds and the influence of Generative AI (GenAI) solutions. To address these challenges, we introduce NAILA, a tool that provides 24/7 autonomous feedback for student exercises. Utilizing GenAI in the form of modern LLMs, NAILA processes student solutions provided in open document formats, evaluating them against teacher-defined model solutions through specialized prompt templates. We conducted an empirical study involving 900+ active students at the University of Duisburg-Essen to assess four main research questions investigating (1) the underlying motivations that drive students to either adopt or reject NAILA, (2) user acceptance by measuring perceived usefulness and ease of use alongside subjective learning progress, (3) how often and how consistently students engage with NAILA, and (4) how using NAILA to receive AI feedback impacts on academic performance compared to human feedback.

</details>

### [149] [From Actions to Understanding: Conformal Interpretability of Temporal Concepts in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19775)
*Trilok Padhi,Ramneet Kaur,Krishiv Agarwal,Adam D. Cobb,Daniel Elenius,Manoj Acharya,Colin Samplawski,Alexander M. Berenbeim,Nathaniel D. Bastian,Susmit Jha,Anirban Roy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于逐步保形预测的框架，用于解释LLM智能体在交互环境中的时序概念演化，通过统计方法标记内部表征的成功/失败，识别对应的潜在方向，并在两个模拟环境中验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）作为自主智能体在推理、规划和行动方面的能力不断增强，但其指导序列行为的内部机制仍然不透明。需要一种方法来解释LLM智能体在交互任务中概念的时间演化，以实现早期失败检测和干预。

Method: 提出了时序任务的保形可解释性框架，结合逐步奖励建模和保形预测，统计地标记模型每一步内部表征的成功或失败。然后在这些表征上训练线性探针，识别时序概念的方向——模型激活空间中对应成功、失败或推理漂移的一致概念的潜在方向。

Result: 在ScienceWorld和AlfWorld两个模拟交互环境中的实验结果表明，这些时序概念是线性可分的，揭示了与任务成功对齐的可解释结构。初步结果显示，通过利用该框架引导模型内部识别的成功方向，可以改善LLM智能体的性能。

Conclusion: 该方法为LLM智能体提供了早期失败检测和干预的原则性方法，为复杂交互环境中可信赖的自主语言模型铺平了道路。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents capable of reasoning, planning, and acting within interactive environments. Despite their growing capability to perform multi-step reasoning and decision-making tasks, internal mechanisms guiding their sequential behavior remain opaque. This paper presents a framework for interpreting the temporal evolution of concepts in LLM agents through a step-wise conformal lens. We introduce the conformal interpretability framework for temporal tasks, which combines step-wise reward modeling with conformal prediction to statistically label model's internal representation at each step as successful or failing. Linear probes are then trained on these representations to identify directions of temporal concepts - latent directions in the model's activation space that correspond to consistent notions of success, failure or reasoning drift. Experimental results on two simulated interactive environments, namely ScienceWorld and AlfWorld, demonstrate that these temporal concepts are linearly separable, revealing interpretable structures aligned with task success. We further show preliminary results on improving an LLM agent's performance by leveraging the proposed framework for steering the identified successful directions inside the model. The proposed approach, thus, offers a principled method for early failure detection as well as intervention in LLM-based agents, paving the path towards trustworthy autonomous language models in complex interactive settings.

</details>


### [150] [The Tool-Overuse Illusion: Why Does LLM Prefer External Tools over Internal Knowledge?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19749)
*Yirong Zeng,Shen You,Yufei Liu,Qunyao Du,Xiao Ding,Yutai Hou,Yuxian Wang,Wu Ning,Haonan Song,Dandan Tu,Bibo Cai,Ting Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了LLM工具过度使用的普遍现象，并提出通过知识感知边界对齐和平衡奖励信号两种方法来缓解这一问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然为LLM配备外部工具能解决内部推理限制，但引入了工具过度使用的现象——在推理过程中不必要地使用工具。这种现象普遍存在但尚未被充分研究。

Method: 采用两种关键视角：1）通过分析不同内部知识可用性区域的工具使用行为，识别"知识认知错觉"，并提出基于直接偏好优化的知识感知认知边界对齐策略；2）通过可视化工具增强训练过程，建立奖励结构与工具使用行为之间的因果关系，并平衡训练中的奖励信号而非仅依赖结果奖励。

Result: 知识感知边界对齐策略将工具使用减少了82.8%同时提高准确性；平衡奖励信号的方法在7B和32B模型上分别减少了66.7%和60.7%的不必要工具调用，且不牺牲准确性。

Conclusion: 工具过度使用是LLM中普遍存在的现象，可通过知识边界对齐和奖励结构优化来有效缓解。论文为理解工具过度使用提供了理论和实践基础。

Abstract: Equipping LLMs with external tools effectively addresses internal reasoning limitations. However, it introduces a critical yet under-explored phenomenon: tool overuse, the unnecessary tool-use during reasoning. In this paper, we first reveal this phenomenon is pervasive across diverse LLMs. We then experimentally elucidate its underlying mechanisms through two key lenses: (1) First, by analyzing tool-use behavior across different internal knowledge availability regions, we identify a \textit{knowledge epistemic illusion}: models misjudge internal knowledge boundaries and fail to accurately perceive their actual knowledge availability. To mitigate this, we propose a knowledge-aware epistemic boundary alignment strategy based on direct preference optimization, which reduces tool usage in by 82.8\% while yielding an accuracy improvement. (2) Second, we establish a causal link between reward structures and tool-use behavior by visualizing the tool-augmented training process. It reveals that \textit{outcome-only rewards} inadvertently encourage tool overuse by rewarding only final correctness, regardless of tool efficiency. To verify this, we balance reward signals during training rather than relying on outcome-only rewards, cutting unnecessary tool calls by 66.7\% (7B) and 60.7\% (32B) without sacrificing accuracy. Finally, we provide theoretical justification in this two lenses to understand tool overuse.

</details>

### [152] [Algorithm Selection with Zero Domain Knowledge via Text Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19753)
*Stefan Szeider*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ZeroFolio：一种无需特征工程的算法选择方法，使用预训练文本嵌入替代手工特征，通过三步流程（序列化、嵌入、选择）在多个问题域中实现优于基于特征的方法的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统算法选择方法依赖手工制作的特征，这需要领域专业知识且难以跨域应用。本文旨在探索使用预训练文本嵌入作为通用表示，避免特征工程，实现跨域算法选择。

Method: 提出ZeroFolio三步方法：1）将实例文件作为纯文本读取；2）使用预训练嵌入模型生成文本表示；3）通过加权k近邻选择算法。关键设计包括逆距离加权、行洗牌和曼哈顿距离。

Result: 在11个ASlib场景（涵盖7个领域）的评估中，ZeroFolio在10个场景中优于基于手工特征的随机森林方法，使用双种子投票时在全部11个场景中获胜，且优势通常显著。当两种选择器都有效时，通过软投票结合嵌入和手工特征可进一步提升性能。

Conclusion: 预训练文本嵌入可作为算法选择的通用表示，无需领域知识或任务特定训练，实现跨域应用。该方法在多个领域超越传统基于特征的方法，展示了特征无关算法选择的潜力。

Abstract: We propose a feature-free approach to algorithm selection that replaces hand-crafted instance features with pretrained text embeddings. Our method, ZeroFolio, proceeds in three steps: it reads the raw instance file as plain text, embeds it with a pretrained embedding model, and selects an algorithm via weighted k-nearest neighbors. The key to our approach is the observation that pretrained embeddings produce representations that distinguish problem instances without any domain knowledge or task-specific training. This allows us to apply the same three-step pipeline (serialize, embed, select) across diverse problem domains with text-based instance formats. We evaluate our approach on 11 ASlib scenarios spanning 7 domains (SAT, MaxSAT, QBF, ASP, CSP, MIP, and graph problems). Our experiments show that this approach outperforms a random forest trained on hand-crafted features in 10 of 11 scenarios with a single fixed configuration, and in all 11 with two-seed voting; the margin is often substantial. Our ablation study shows that inverse-distance weighting, line shuffling, and Manhattan distance are the key design choices. On scenarios where both selectors are competitive, combining embeddings with hand-crafted features via soft voting yields further improvements.

Abstract: Anti-money laundering (AML) transaction monitoring generates large volumes of alerts that must be rapidly triaged by investigators under strict audit and governance constraints. While large language models (LLMs) can summarize heterogeneous evidence and draft rationales, unconstrained generation is risky in regulated workflows due to hallucinations, weak provenance, and explanations that are not faithful to the underlying decision. We propose an explainable AML triage framework that treats triage as an evidence-constrained decision process. Our method combines (i) retrieval-augmented evidence bundling from policy/typology guidance, customer context, alert triggers, and transaction subgraphs, (ii) a structured LLM output contract that requires explicit citations and separates supporting from contradicting or missing evidence, and (iii) counterfactual checks that validate whether minimal, plausible perturbations lead to coherent changes in both the triage recommendation and its rationale. We evaluate on public synthetic AML benchmarks and simulators and compare against rules, tabular and graph machine-learning baselines, and LLM-only/RAG-only variants. Results show that evidence grounding substantially improves auditability and reduces numerical and policy hallucination errors, while counterfactual validation further increases decision-linked explainability and robustness, yielding the best overall triage performance (PR-AUC 0.75; Escalate F1 0.62) and strong provenance and faithfulness metrics (citation validity 0.98; evidence support 0.88; counterfactual faithfulness 0.76). These findings indicate that governed, verifiable LLM systems can provide practical decision support for AML triage without sacrificing compliance requirements for traceability and defensibility.

Abstract: We present ThermoQA, a benchmark of 293 open-ended engineering thermodynamics problems in three tiers: property lookups (110 Q), component analysis (101 Q), and full cycle analysis (82 Q). Ground truth is computed programmatically from CoolProp 7.2.0, covering water, R-134a, and variable-cp air. Six frontier LLMs are evaluated across three independent runs each. Our findings highlight the importance of feature selection as a regularization technique and demonstrate that sparse lexical features remain complementary to dense representations for specialized clinical text classification under severe class imbalance.

### [156] [Inference Headroom Ratio: A Diagnostic and Control Framework for Inference Stability Under Constraint](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19760)
*Robert Reinertsen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出并评估了推理余量比(IHR)，这是一个用于表征受限决策系统中推理稳定性的无量纲诊断指标，通过模拟实验验证了IHR作为量化风险指标、稳定性边界敏感指示器和可行控制变量的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI系统在分布偏移和约束条件下运行时，缺乏能够量化系统级推理稳定性边界的指标。现有性能、漂移和不确定性指标主要关注输出层面，无法有效估计系统在明显故障前的剩余推理余量。

Method: 提出推理余量比(IHR)作为诊断指标，形式化定义了系统有效推理能力C与环境不确定性及约束负载(U+K)之间的关系。通过三个受控模拟实验：1)验证IHR与崩溃概率的逻辑曲线关系；2)测试IHR对环境噪声下稳定性边界的敏感性；3)评估IHR作为控制变量对系统稳定性的调节效果。

Result: 实验结果表明：1)IHR与崩溃概率呈良好拟合的逻辑曲线关系，估计临界阈值IHR*≈1.19；2)IHR能敏感指示环境噪声下的推理稳定性边界；3)主动调节IHR可将系统崩溃率从79.4%降至58.7%，IHR方差降低70.4%。

Conclusion: IHR可作为标准性能、漂移和不确定性指标的系统级补充，为在分布偏移和约束条件下运行的AI系统提供量化推理稳定性边界和估计剩余推理余量的能力。

Abstract: We present a simulation-based evaluation of the Inference Headroom Ratio (IHR), a dimensionless diagnostic quantity for characterizing inference stability in constrained decision systems. IHR formalizes the relationship between a system's effective inferential capacity C and the combined uncertainty and constraint load U + K imposed by its operating environment, and is intended to capture proximity to an inference stability boundary rather than output-level performance. Across three controlled experiments, we show that IHR functions as: (1) a quantifiable risk indicator whose relationship to collapse probability follows a well-fitted logistic curve with estimated critical threshold IHR* approx. 1.19, (2) a sensitive indicator of proximity to the inference stability boundary under environmental noise, and (3) a viable control variable whose active regulation reduces system collapse rate from 79.4% to 58.7% and IHR variance by 70.4% across 300 Monte Carlo runs. These results position IHR as a prospective, system-level complement to standard performance, drift, and uncertainty metrics, enabling estimation of remaining inferential margin before overt failure in AI systems operating under distributional shift and constraint.

### [157] [EvoForest: A Novel Machine-Learning Paradigm via Open-Ended Evolution of Computational Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19761)
*Kamer Ali Yuksel,Hassan Sawaf*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: EvoForest是一个混合神经符号系统，通过端到端的开放式进化来发现计算结构，在结构化预测问题上超越了传统参数优化方法


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统机器学习主要围绕参数优化，但在结构化预测问题中，主要瓶颈不是参数拟合，而是发现应该从数据中计算什么。当目标函数不可微分、评估基于交叉验证、需要可解释性或持续适应时，识别正确的变换、统计量、不变性等计算结构至关重要。

Method: EvoForest是一个混合神经符号系统，在共享的有向无环图中联合进化可重用的计算结构、可调用函数族和可训练的低维连续组件。系统包含中间节点存储替代实现、可调用节点编码可重用变换族、输出节点定义候选预测计算，以及可通过梯度下降优化的全局参数。系统使用轻量级Ridge回归读取器评估计算，并生成结构化反馈指导未来的LLM驱动突变。

Result: 在2025年ADIA Lab结构性断点挑战赛中，EvoForest经过600步进化后达到了94.13%的ROC-AUC，超过了公开报道的获胜分数90.14%（使用相同评估协议）。

Conclusion: EvoForest展示了通过开放式进化发现计算结构的有效性，为结构化预测问题提供了一种超越传统参数优化范式的解决方案，特别适用于非可微分目标、交叉验证评估、需要可解释性和持续适应的场景。

Abstract: Modern machine learning is still largely organized around a single recipe: choose a parameterized model family and optimize its weights. Although highly successful, this paradigm is too narrow for many structured prediction problems, where the main bottleneck is not parameter fitting but discovering what should be computed from the data. Success often depends on identifying the right transformations, statistics, invariances, interaction structures, temporal summaries, gates, or nonlinear compositions, especially when objectives are non-differentiable, evaluation is cross-validation-based, interpretability matters, or continual adaptation is required. We present EvoForest, a hybrid neuro-symbolic system for end-to-end open-ended evolution of computation. Rather than merely generating features, EvoForest jointly evolves reusable computational structure, callable function families, and trainable low-dimensional continuous components inside a shared directed acyclic graph. Intermediate nodes store alternative implementations, callable nodes encode reusable transformation families such as projections, gates, and activations, output nodes define candidate predictive computations, and persistent global parameters can be refined by gradient descent. For each graph configuration, EvoForest evaluates the discovered computation and uses a lightweight Ridge-based readout to score the resulting representation against a non-differentiable cross-validation target. The evaluator also produces structured feedback that guides future LLM-driven mutations. In the 2025 ADIA Lab Structural Break Challenge, EvoForest reached 94.13% ROC-AUC after 600 evolution steps, exceeding the publicly reported winning score of 90.14% under the same evaluation protocol.

</details>

*Yifei Wang,Tianlin Li,Xiaohan Zhang,Xiaoyu Zhang,Wei Ma,Mingfei Cheng,Li Pan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PrecisionDiff是一个自动化差分测试框架，用于系统检测不同精度配置下大型语言模型的行为不一致问题，特别是在对齐验证任务中发现精度导致的越狱分歧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在不同数值精度配置（如bfloat16、float16、int16、int8）下部署时，存在难以检测的微小行为不一致问题，现有评估方法往往忽略这些精度导致的差异。

Method: PrecisionDiff通过生成精度敏感的测试输入，并进行跨精度比较分析，系统性地检测精度引起的行为分歧。框架包括自动化测试生成和差分测试机制。

Result: 实验结果显示，精度导致的行为分歧在多个开源对齐LLM和精度设置中普遍存在，PrecisionDiff在检测这些问题上显著优于传统测试方法。

Conclusion: PrecisionDiff实现了自动化精度敏感测试生成，有助于有效的部署前评估，并在训练过程中提高精度鲁棒性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed under diverse numerical precision configurations, including standard floating-point formats (e.g., bfloat16 and float16) and quantized integer formats (e.g., int16 and int8), to meet efficiency and resource constraints. However, minor inconsistencies between LLMs of different precisions are difficult to detect and are often overlooked by existing evaluation methods. In this paper, we present PrecisionDiff, an automated differential testing framework for systematically detecting precision-induced behavioral disagreements in LLMs. PrecisionDiff generates precision-sensitive test inputs and performs cross-precision comparative analysis to uncover subtle divergences that remain hidden under conventional testing strategies. To demonstrate its practical significance, we instantiate PrecisionDiff on the alignment verification task, where precision-induced disagreements manifest as jailbreak divergence-inputs that are rejected under one precision may produce harmful responses under another. Experimental results show that such behavioral disagreements are widespread across multiple open-source aligned LLMs and precision settings, and that PrecisionDiff significantly outperforms vanilla testing methods in detecting these issues. Our work enables automated precision-sensitive test generation, facilitating effective pre-deployment evaluation and improving precision robustness during training.

These accounts often function as mechanism sketches: rich in conceptual detail, yet lacking the technical specifications and operational constraints required to run as executable systems. We present a generative actor-based modelling workflow for "rendering" these sketches as runnable actor - environment simulations using the Concordia simulation library. In Concordia, actors operate by predictive pattern completion: an operation on natural language strings that generates a suffix which describes the actor's intended action from a prefix containing memories of their past and observations of the present. We render the theories of cognitive dissonance (Festinger 1957), self-consistency (Aronson 1969), and self-perception (Bem 1972) as distinct decision logics that populate and process the prefix through theory-specific sequences of reasoning steps. We evaluate these implementations across classic psychological experiments. Our implementations generate behavioural patterns consistent with known results from the original empirical literature. However, we find that achieving stable reproduction requires resolving the inherent underdetermination of the verbal accounts and the conflicts between modern linguistic priors and historical experimental assumptions. And, we document how this manual process of iterative model "stabilisation" surfaces specific operational and socio-ecological dependencies that were largely undocumented in the original verbal accounts. Ultimately, we argue that the manual stabilisation process itself should be regarded as a core part of the methodology functioning to clarify situational and representational commitments needed to generate characteristic effects.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粗糙集理论通过不可分辨关系或粒化关系近似目标概念来建模不确定性，捕捉观测分辨率有限导致的模糊性。本书旨在提供粗糙集模型的系统性综述和分类框架，而非专注于特征约简和规则归纳等具体算法。

Abstract: Rough set theory models uncertainty by approximating target concepts through lower and upper sets induced by indiscernibility, or more generally, by granulation relations in data tables. This perspective captures vagueness caused by limited observational resolution and supports set-theoretic reasoning about what can be determined with certainty and what remains only possible. This book is written as a map of models. Rather than developing a single algorithmic pipeline in depth, it provides a systematic survey of the main rough set paradigms and their extension routes. More specifically, representative variants are organized according to (i) the underlying granulation mechanism, such as equivalence-based, tolerance-based, covering-based, neighborhood-based, and probabilistic approximations, and (ii) the uncertainty semantics attached to data and relations, such as crisp, fuzzy, intuitionistic fuzzy, neutrosophic, and plithogenic settings. The book also explains how each choice changes the form of approximations and the interpretation of boundary regions. Throughout the book, small illustrative examples are used to clarify modeling intent and typical use cases in classification and decision support. Finally, an important clarification of scope should be noted. Since the main purpose of this book is to provide a map of models, the Abstract and Introduction should not lead readers to expect that feature reduction and rule induction are primary objectives. Although these topics are central in the rough set literature, they are treated here mainly as motivating applications and as entry points to the broader research landscape. The principal aim of the book is to survey and position rough set models and their extensions in a systematic and coherent manner.

### [162] [Skyline-First Traversal as a Control Mechanism for Multi-Criteria Graph Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19807)
*Nicolas Tacheny*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于帕累托几何的确定性搜索框架，在多准则图遍历中仅使用帕累托支配关系就能驱动搜索调度和终止，无需外部启发式、标量化或概率模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多准则图遍历方法中，帕累托支配仅用于被动角色（如剪枝或排序），而搜索调度和终止需要依赖外部机制（启发式、标量化或基于群体的探索）。本文旨在证明在特定约束条件下，仅凭帕累托几何就足以驱动搜索过程。

Result: 建立了确定性势能下降、通过支配覆盖的认证终止、成本网格几何诱导的层宽均匀界限，以及天际线内的贪婪成本空间分散。该框架无需标量化、启发式指导或概率模型。

Abstract: In multi-criteria graph traversal, paths are compared via Pareto dominance, an ordering that identifies which paths are non-dominated, but says nothing about which path to expand next or when the search may stop. As a result, existing approaches rely on external mechanisms-heuristics, scalarization, or population-based exploration while Pareto dominance remains confined to passive roles such as pruning or ranking.
  This paper shows that, under constrained cost models, finite cost grids, Markovian transitions, and a nonzero progress measure, Pareto geometry alone is sufficient to drive both scheduling and termination. We show that extracting exclusively from the first Pareto layer, the skyline, induces a deterministic descent in a discrete completion potential, ensuring monotone progress toward solution completion. In parallel, a vector lower-bound certificate provides a stopping condition that guarantees dominance coverage of all remaining traversals without requiring a predefined number of solutions.
  Our analysis establishes deterministic potential descent, certified termination via dominance coverage, a uniform bound on layer width induced by cost-grid geometry, and greedy cost-space dispersion within the skyline. The resulting framework operates without scalarization, heuristic guidance, or probabilistic models, and repositions Pareto dominance from a passive filter to a deterministic driver of search.

### [163] [MIRROR: A Hierarchical Benchmark for Metacognitive Calibration in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19809)
*Jason Z Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估大语言模型是否能够利用自我认知来做出更好的决策，这对于自主AI系统的安全部署具有重要意义。

Result: 发现两个关键现象：1) 组合性自我预测普遍失败，模型无法预测自身在多领域任务的表现；2) 模型具有高于随机但非完美的领域特定自我认知，但无法将其转化为适当的行动选择，外部元认知控制能将自信失败率降低70-76%。

Abstract: We introduce MIRROR, a benchmark comprising eight experiments across four metacognitive levels that evaluates whether large language models can use self-knowledge to make better decisions. We evaluate 16 models from 8 labs across approximately 250,000 evaluation instances using five independent behavioral measurement channels. Core experiments are run across the full model roster; experiments with specialized infrastructure requirements report explicitly marked model subsets. We find two phenomena with direct implications for agentic deployment: (1) compositional self-prediction fails universally -- the Compositional Calibration Error ranges from 0.500 to 0.943 on the original 15-model Exp3-v1 set (and 0.434 to 0.758 on the balanced 16-model Exp3-v2 expansion), indicating that models cannot predict their own performance on multi-domain tasks, and (2) models exhibit above-chance but imperfect domain-specific self-knowledge yet systematically fail to translate even this partial awareness into appropriate agentic action-selection -- external metacognitive control reduces the Confident Failure Rate from 0.600 to 0.143 (76% reduction at temperature 0; mean 70% at temperature 0.7 across 5 models from 4 labs). Providing models with their own calibration scores produces no significant improvement (p > 0.05); only architectural constraint is effective. This suggests that external metacognitive scaffolding -- not improved self-knowledge -- is the path to safer autonomous AI systems. Code, data, and Croissant metadata will be released publicly with the benchmark.

### [164] [The Existential Theory of Research: Why Discovery Is Hard](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19810)
*Angshul Majumdar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出"存在性研究理论"(ETR)框架，论证科学发现不可能通过优化表示、数据和算法而变得任意简单，因为表示、观察和计算三个维度存在根本性约束和权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨科学发现是否可以通过选择合适表示、收集足够数据和部署强大算法而变得任意简单，挑战当前对大数据和人工智能能解决所有科学问题的乐观预期。

Method: 提出"存在性研究理论"(ETR)形式化框架，将发现建模为在表示、观察和计算约束下恢复结构化解释的过程，结合稀疏表示的不确定性原理、高维恢复的样本复杂度界限和精确推理的计算复杂性进行分析。

Result: 证明表示、观察和计算三个维度无法同时优化：没有方法能保证普遍简单的解释、任意压缩的观察和高效的精确推理；表示不匹配会放大内在简单性为表观复杂性；引入量化发现难度的不确定性泛函。

Conclusion: 科学困难不是偶然的，而是推理几何和复杂性的结构后果，存在表示、观察和计算之间的根本权衡，科学发现不可能变得任意简单。

Abstract: Can scientific discovery be made arbitrarily easy by choosing the right representation, collecting enough data, and deploying sufficiently powerful algorithms? This paper argues that the answer is fundamentally negative. We introduce the Existential Theory of Research (ETR), a formal framework that models discovery as the recovery of structured explanations under constraints of representation, observation, and computation. Within this framework, we show that these three components cannot be simultaneously optimized: no method can guarantee universally simple explanations, arbitrarily compressed observations, and efficient exact inference. This limitation is not model-specific, but arises from a synthesis of uncertainty principles in sparse representation, sample complexity bounds in high-dimensional recovery, and the computational hardness of exact inference. We further show that representation mismatch alone can inflate intrinsic simplicity into apparent complexity, rendering otherwise tractable problems observationally and computationally prohibitive. To quantify these effects, we introduce an uncertainty functional that captures the joint difficulty of discovery. The results suggest that scientific difficulty is not accidental, but a structural consequence of the geometry and complexity of inference.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解道路使用者如何解决空间共享冲突对于交通安全和自动驾驶车辆的安全部署至关重要。现有模型仅捕捉了交互的特定方面（如显式通信），缺乏理论基础的建模框架。

Method: 扩展先前开发的基于主动推理的驾驶员行为模型，模拟两个智能体的交互行为。模型捕捉了三种互补的不确定性降低机制：1）通过直接行为耦合的隐式通信；2）依赖规范性期望（停车标志、优先规则等）；3）显式通信。

Result: 在简化的交叉口场景中，规范性和显式通信线索可以增加成功解决冲突的可能性。但这依赖于智能体按预期行事。当其他智能体（有意或无意地）违反规范性期望或传递误导信息时，依赖这些线索可能导致碰撞。

Conclusion: 主动推理为建模道路使用者交互提供了一个新颖的框架，该框架也可应用于其他领域。研究揭示了在交互中平衡不同通信机制的重要性，特别是在存在期望违反或误导信息的情况下。

Abstract: Understanding how road users resolve space-sharing conflicts is important both for traffic safety and the safe deployment of autonomous vehicles. While existing models have captured specific aspects of such interactions (e.g., explicit communication), a theoretically-grounded computational framework has been lacking. In this paper, we extend a previously developed active inference-based driver behavior model to simulate interactive behavior of two agents. Our model captures three complementary mechanisms for uncertainty reduction in interaction: (i) implicit communication via direct behavioral coupling, (ii) reliance on normative expectations (stop signs, priority rules, etc.), and (iii) explicit communication. In a simplified intersection scenario, we show that normative and explicit communication cues can increase the likelihood of a successful conflict resolution. However, this relies on agents acting as expected. In situations where another agent (intentionally or unintentionally) violates normative expectations or communicates misleading information, reliance on these cues may induce collisions. These findings illustrate how active inference can provide a novel framework for modeling road user interactions which is also applicable in other fields.

</details>


### [167] [Deconstructing Superintelligence: Identity, Self-Modification and Différance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19845)
*Elija Perrier*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文探讨人工智能自我修改的理论极限，指出当自我修改扩展到其外部补充时，经典自指结构会崩溃，并用量子代数形式化这一现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究人工智能自我修改的理论基础，揭示当自我修改试图包含其外部补充时产生的结构性问题，这关系到超级智能的可行性。

Method: 使用结合算子代数 $\mathcal{A}$ 形式化系统，定义更新算子 $\hat{U}$、判别算子 $\hat{D}$ 和自表示算子 $\hat{R}$，将补充识别为 $\mathrm{Comm}(\hat{U})$，通过展开定理分析非对易性的传播。

Result: 发现 $[\hat{U},\hat{R}]$ 通过 $[\hat{U},\hat{D}]$ 分解，非对易性普遍传播；说谎者悖论表现为对易子崩溃 $[\hat{T},Π_L]=0$，A类自我修改在系统尺度上实现相同崩溃。

Conclusion: 自我修改在扩展到其外部补充时会导致结构崩溃，这与普里斯特的包含模式和德里达的延异理论一致，揭示了超级智能自我修改的根本限制。

Abstract: Self-modification is often taken as constitutive of artificial superintelligence (SI), yet modification is a relative action requiring a supplement outside the operation. When self-modification extends to this supplement, the classical self-referential structure collapses. We formalise this on an associative operator algebra $\mathcal{A}$ with update $\hat{U}$, discrimination $\hat{D}$, and self-representation $\hat{R}$, identifying the supplement with $\mathrm{Comm}(\hat{U})$; an expansion theorem shows that $[\hat{U},\hat{R}]$ decomposes through $[\hat{U},\hat{D}]$, so non-commutation generically propagates. The liar paradox appears as a commutator collapse $[\hat{T},Π_L]=0$, and class $\mathbf{A}$ self-modification realises the same collapse at system scale, yielding a structure coinciding with Priest's inclosure schema and Derrida's diffèrance.

### [168] [Learning When Not to Decide: A Framework for Overcoming Factual Presumptuousness in AI Adjudication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19895)
*Mohamed Afane,Emily Robitschek,Derek Ouyang,Daniel E. Ho*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究AI在法律应用中的武断性问题，特别是在失业保险裁决中，提出SPEC框架来改善AI在证据不足时的决策准确性


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI系统存在武断性问题，即在信息不足时仍提供自信的答案。这在法律应用中尤为严重，特别是失业保险裁决领域，AI系统已快速集成，而额外事实调查问题成为影响数百万申请人的系统中最显著的瓶颈

Method: 1. 与科罗拉多州劳工和就业部合作获取官方培训材料，设计系统变化信息完整性的新基准；2. 评估四个领先AI平台；3. 引入SPEC框架，要求在任何决定前明确识别缺失信息

Result: 1. 标准RAG方法在信息不足时平均准确率仅为15%；2. 高级提示方法提高了不确定案例的准确性，但过度纠正，甚至在明确案例中也拒绝决策；3. SPEC框架达到89%的整体准确率，同时在证据不足时适当推迟决策

Conclusion: AI在法律应用中的武断性是系统性的但可解决。SPEC框架表明，通过要求明确识别缺失信息，AI可以可靠地支持而非取代人类判断，特别是在需要足够证据才能做出决策的领域

Abstract: A well-known limitation of AI systems is presumptuousness: the tendency of AI systems to provide confident answers when information may be lacking. This challenge is particularly acute in legal applications, where a core task for attorneys, judges, and administrators is to determine whether evidence is sufficient to reach a conclusion. We study this problem in the important setting of unemployment insurance adjudication, which has seen rapid integration of AI systems and where the question of additional fact-finding poses the most significant bottleneck for a system that affects millions of applicants annually. First, through a collaboration with the Colorado Department of Labor and Employment, we secure rare access to official training materials and guidance to design a novel benchmark that systematically varies in information completeness. Second, we evaluate four leading AI platforms and show that standard RAG-based approaches achieve an average of only 15% accuracy when information is insufficient. Third, advanced prompting methods improve accuracy on inconclusive cases but over-correct, withholding decisions even on clear cases. Fourth, we introduce a structured framework requiring explicit identification of missing information before any determination (SPEC, Structured Prompting for Evidence Checklists). SPEC achieves 89% overall accuracy, while appropriately deferring when evidence is insufficient -- demonstrating that presumptuousness in legal AI is systematic but addressable, and that doing so is a necessary step towards systems that reliably support, rather than supplant, human judgment wherever decisions must await sufficient evidence.

### [169] [What Makes a Good AI Review? Concern-Level Diagnostics for AI Peer Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19998)
*Ming Jin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出"关注对齐"诊断框架，在关注层面而非仅结论层面评估AI审稿系统，通过匹配图分析关注检测、校准和优先级对齐问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI审稿评估方法主要依赖结论一致性，但这种方法不够充分，无法审计系统识别哪些关注点、如何优先排序这些关注点，以及这些优先级是否与最终评估的审稿理由一致。

Method: 提出关注对齐框架，核心数据结构是匹配图——官方关注与AI生成关注之间的二分对齐图，标注匹配类型、严重性和反驳后处理。由此推导出从二元准确性到关注检测、结论分层行为、决策感知校准和反驳感知分解的评估阶梯。

Result: 在四个公共AI审稿系统的六种配置试点研究中发现：检测本身不能决定审稿质量；校准通常是主要约束。系统能检测到相当比例的官方关注，但大多数将25-55%被接受论文的关注标记为决定性，而实际上没有官方关注被当作决定性障碍。相同的总体结论准确性可能掩盖拒绝倾向行为与低召回率特征。

Conclusion: 贡献了一个可重复使用的评估框架，用于审计AI审稿员识别哪些关注点、如何权衡这些关注点，以及这些优先级是否与影响论文最终评估的审稿理由一致。大多数系统不直接输出接受/拒绝结论，从审稿语气推断结论对方法敏感，这强化了需要关注层面的诊断方法。

Abstract: Evaluating AI-generated reviews by verdict agreement is widely recognized as insufficient, yet current alternatives rarely audit which concerns a system identifies, how it prioritizes them, or whether those priorities align with the review rationale that shaped the final assessment. We propose concern alignment, a diagnostic framework that evaluates AI reviews at the concern level rather than only at the verdict level. The framework's core data structure is the match graph, a bipartite alignment between official and AI-generated concerns annotated with match type, severity, and post-rebuttal treatment. From this artifact we derive an evaluation ladder that moves from binary accuracy to concern detection, verdict-stratified behavior, decision-aware calibration, and rebuttal-aware decomposition. In a pilot study of four public AI review systems evaluated in six configurations, concern-level analysis suggests that detection alone does not determine review quality; calibration is often the binding constraint. Systems detect non-trivial fractions of official concerns yet most mark 25--55% of concerns on accepted papers as decisive, where, under our operationalization, no official concern on accepted papers was treated as a decisive blocker. Identical overall verdict accuracy can conceal reject-heavy behavior versus low-recall profiles, and low full-review false decisive rates can partly reflect concern dilution rather than calibrated prioritization. Most systems do not emit a native accept/reject, and inferring it from review tone is method-sensitive, reinforcing the need for concern-level diagnostics that remain stable across inference choices. The contribution is a reusable evaluation framework for auditing which concerns AI reviewers identify, how they weight them, and whether those priorities align with the review rationale that informed the paper's final assessment.

### [170] [HiPO: Hierarchical Preference Optimization for Adaptive Reasoning in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20140)
*Darsh Kachroo,Adriana Caraeni,Arjun Prasaath Anbazhagan,Brennan Lagasse,Kevin Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HiPO是一种改进的DPO方法，通过将回答分解为推理段（查询澄清、推理步骤、答案）并计算各段加权损失，解决了DPO在复杂推理任务中缺乏细粒度反馈的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DPO在复杂推理任务中存在局限性，它优化的是整个回答的偏好概率，缺乏对多步推理中各个子部分的细粒度反馈。现有方法要么擅长稳定偏好学习（如DPO变体），要么擅长结构化推理（如多智能体RL框架），但未能结合这两者的优势。

Method: 提出HiPO（分层偏好优化），将回答分解为推理段：查询澄清和上下文、推理步骤、答案。计算损失时采用各段DPO损失的加权和，实现段特异性训练，同时保持DPO的计算效率和训练稳定性。

Result: 在Math Stack Exchange偏好数据集上对多个7B LLM进行微调，HiPO训练的模型在各种常见数学基准测试中优于DPO模型，并且GPT-4评估显示其具有更好的组织性、逻辑流程和一致性。

Conclusion: HiPO通过分层方法有效结合了稳定偏好学习和结构化推理的优势，在复杂推理任务中显著提升了模型性能，同时保持了训练效率和稳定性。

Abstract: Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) is an effective framework for aligning large language models with human preferences, but it struggles with complex reasoning tasks. DPO optimizes for the likelihood of generating preferred over dispreferred responses in their entirety and lacks the granularity to provide feedback on subsections of many-step solutions typical of reasoning tasks. Existing methods excel at either stable preference learning (e.g., DPO variants like KTO and RSO) or structured reasoning (e.g., ReMA's multi-agent RL framework, Tree of Thoughts), but fail to merge these complementary strengths. We propose HiPO (Hierarchical Preference Optimization), an extension of DPO that separates responses into reasoning segments (query clarification and context, reasoning steps, and answer) and computes loss as a weighted sum of the DPO loss for each segment. Our approach enables segment-specific training while maintaining DPO's computational efficiency and training stability. We demonstrate that for multiple 7B LLMs fine-tuned using HiPO and DPO on the Math Stack Exchange preference dataset, the models trained with HiPO outperform the others on a variety of common math benchmarks and achieve greater organization, logical flow, and consistency as measured by GPT-4.1.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Mol-Debate生成范式，通过迭代的生成-辩论-精炼循环实现动态推理。采用面向视角的编排机制解决关键挑战：开发者-辩论者冲突、全局-局部结构推理、静态-动态集成。

Abstract: Text-guided molecular design is a key capability for AI-driven drug discovery, yet it remains challenging to map sequential natural-language instructions with non-linear molecular structures under strict chemical constraints. Most existing approaches, including RAG, CoT prompting, and fine-tuning or RL, emphasize a small set of ad-hoc reasoning perspectives implemented in a largely one-shot generation pipeline. In contrast, real-world drug discovery relies on dynamic, multi-perspective critique and iterative refinement to reconcile semantic intent with structural feasibility. Motivated by this, we propose Mol-Debate, a generation paradigm that enables such dynamic reasoning through an iterative generate-debate-refine loop. We further characterize key challenges in this paradigm and address them through perspective-oriented orchestration, including developer-debater conflict, global-local structural reasoning, and static-dynamic integration. Experiments demonstrate that Mol-Debate achieves state-of-the-art performance against strong general and chemical baselines, reaching 59.82% exact match on ChEBI-20 and 50.52% weighted success rate on S$^2$-Bench. Our code is available at https://github.com/wyuzh/Mol-Debate.

Recent Large Language Model (LLM)-based approaches introduce richer semantic signals, but still suffer from a restricted feature space due to fixed generation patterns and from the absence of feedback from the learning objective. MALMAS decomposes the generation process into agents with distinct responsibilities, and a Router Agent activates an appropriate subset of agents per iteration, further broadening exploration of the feature space.   <summary>Details</summary>
